## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (rate laws / kinetic ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is explicitly the time-derivative of a chemical concentration A, which is the standard setup for kinetic rate laws written as ordinary differential equations. With features limited to t and A, the most likely models are elementary-order rate laws, autocatalytic/equilibrium relaxations, or time-varying rate coefficients k(t).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate depletion, e.g., saturated catalyst or constant-flux feed/decay)
- First-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive/thermal decomposition, pseudo-first-order kinetics)
- Second-order decay (dimerization/bi-molecular): dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (elementary bimolecular consumption with identical reactants lumped into A)
- nth-order power-law rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical overall reaction order when mechanism is not elementary)
- Equilibrium relaxation (linear driving force): dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to steady-state/equilibrium concentration c1)
- Autocatalytic / self-accelerating with limiting capacity: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (autocatalysis or growth-with-depletion where A promotes its own production but is limited)
- Reversible-like net rate with nonlinear forward term: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 + c2 (net consumption with constant source/back-reaction lumped as c2)
- Time-varying first-order (exponentially changing conditions): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(c1 * t) * A (k(t) changes due to heating, activation, or catalyst conditioning)
- Time-varying first-order (power-law drift): dA_dt = -c0 * (t + c1)**c2 * A (rate coefficient changes as a power of time, e.g., catalyst deactivation/aging effects)
- Time-varying first-order (hyperbolic decay of activity): dA_dt = -c0 / (t + c1) * A (rate slows over time due to depletion of active sites or progressive inhibition)
- Mixed-order / inhibition-like rational form: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (apparent saturation/inhibition with respect to A without introducing new species variables)
- Stretched-exponential-in-time modulation: dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t**c2) * A (time-dependent activity or accessibility following stretched-exponential relaxation)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- If dA_dt is approximately constant and negative over a range, a zero-order term (-c0) is indicated (rate independent of A).
- If dA_dt scales linearly with A (plot dA_dt vs A is near a line through origin), first-order kinetics (-c0*A) is likely.
- If dA_dt scales with A**2 (linearity in dA_dt vs A**2), a bimolecular/second-order consumption mechanism is suggested.
- Curvature on a log(-dA_dt) vs log(A) plot suggests a non-integer or changing apparent order (use -c0*A**c1).
- A nonzero intercept in dA_dt vs A (i.e., dA_dt≈0 at A=c1) indicates relaxation toward a steady level (use -c0*(A-c1)).
- Sign changes in dA_dt across A imply a stable fixed point; structures like -c0*(A-c1) or c0*A*(c1-A) encode attraction to an equilibrium/limit.
- Systematic time-dependence of effective rate constant k_eff(t) inferred from -(dA_dt)/A motivates explicit k(t) modulation (e.g., exp(c*t), (t+c1)**c2, or 1/(t+c1)).
- Early-time induction or late-time slowing that cannot be explained by A alone often fits a decaying activity factor multiplying A (e.g., exp(-c*t**p)*A).

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK5)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_f*A**c2
Candidate formulas: 77

GT is the fixed function (independent of \(t\)):
\[
0.5229500625821207\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.3254156367450257\,\sqrt{A}.
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of \(t\) after parameter choice, (ii) have exactly two power terms in \(A\): \(A^{1/3}\) and \(\sqrt A\), with the specific coefficients above, and (iii) have no extra constant, log/sin/exp/rational-in-\(A\) residue unless it can be identically zeroed.

Below, each candidate either can be reduced to the GT by setting some parameters (typically killing extra terms), or cannot.

1. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2(c3+t)^{c4}\sin(\cdots)\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0=-0.3254156367\), \(c1=0.5229500626\). Matches (up to \(|A|^{1/3}\) vs \(A^{1/3}\); for real-valued equivalence on all real \(A\), GT isn’t real for \(A<0\) anyway; on the natural domain \(A\ge0\) they coincide).
2. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\): set \(c2=0\); choose \(c0=0.5229500626\), \(c1=-0.3254156367\). Matches.
3. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\sin(Ac3+c4)\): set \(c2=0\); choose \(c0=-0.3254156367\), \(c1=0.5229500626\). Matches.
4. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + c2\sin(c3\log(c4 e^{Ac5}+1)+c6)\): set \(c2=0\); choose \(c0,c1\) as in (2). Matches.
5. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + \frac{Ac1}{c2 t+c3} + c4|A|^{1/3} + \frac{c5}{c2 t+c3}\): to remove \(t\)-dependence for all \(t\), set \(c1=0,c5=0\) (or \(c2=0\) but then still \(A\)-term remains unless \(c1=0\)). Then it reduces to \(\sqrt(A)c0+c4|A|^{1/3}\). Choose \(c0=-0.3254\), \(c4=0.52295\). Matches.
6. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + \frac{Ac2}{c3 t+c4} + \frac{c5}{c3 t+c4}\): similarly set \(c2=0,c5=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\) as in (2). Matches.
7. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\log(c3 t+1)|A|^{c4}\): must eliminate the \(t\)-dependent log term for all \(t\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\) as in (3). Matches.
8. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + A^{c2}c3\log(c4 t+1)\): eliminate \(t\)-dependence by setting \(c3=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\) as in (2). Matches.
9. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\frac{|A|^{c3}}{c4+|A|^{c3}}\): the rational term depends on \(A\) and cannot equal 0 for all \(A\) unless \(c2=0\). Set \(c2=0\); then choose \(c0,c1\) as in (3). Matches.
10. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + A^{c2}c3/(A^{c2}+c4)\): kill extra \(A\)-dependent rational term by \(c3=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\) as in (2). Matches.
11. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\log(c3 e^{c4 t}|A|^{c5}+1)\): kill log term by \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
12. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\sin(c3\log(c4|A|+1)+c5)\): kill sine term by \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
13. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2 e^{c3 t}\log(c4 t+1)\): kill \(t\)-term by \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
14. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\): to match GT (no constant term), need \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
15. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + c2\): set \(c2=0\); choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
16. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + \frac{Ac2}{Ac3+c4} + \frac{c5}{Ac3+c4}\): extra rational-in-\(A\) terms must vanish for all \(A\): set \(c2=0,c5=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
17. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + \frac{Ac1}{Ac2+c3} + c4|A|^{1/3} + \frac{c5}{Ac2+c3}\): kill rational terms by \(c1=0,c5=0\). Then choose \(c0,c4\). Matches.
18. \(\frac{\sqrt(A)A^{c0}c1}{A^{c0}+c2} + \frac{\sqrt(A)c3}{A^{c0}+c2} + \frac{A^{c0}c4}{A^{c0}+c2}\): this is a nontrivial rational combination; easiest is to force all three terms to 0 by setting \(c1=c3=c4=0\), but then expression is identically 0 and cannot equal GT. There is no way to make it exactly a linear combination of \(\sqrt A\) and \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\) because everything is divided by \(A^{c0}+c2\). So cannot match.
19. \(\frac{\sqrt(A)c0}{A^{c1}+c2} + \frac{A^{c3}c4}{A^{c1}+c2}\): same obstruction: common denominator \(A^{c1}+c2\) prevents it from being a pure sum of two power terms for all \(A\) unless denominator is constant 1, which is impossible for all \(A\) (cannot make \(A^{c1}\) constant for all \(A\)). Cannot match.
20. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t^{c3}} + c4|A|^{1/3}\): must remove \(t\)-dependent \(A\)-linear term: set \(c1=0\). Then choose \(c0,c4\). Matches.
21. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + A c2 e^{c3 t^{c4}}\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
22. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2\max(0,A)\): extra piecewise \(A\) term must vanish: set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
23. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + c2\log(c3 e^{\sqrt(A)c4 + c5 t}+1)\): log term depends on \(A\) and/or \(t\); only safe removal is \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
24. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + A c1 e^{c2/(c3+t)} + c4|A|^{1/3}\): remove \(t\)-dependent \(A\) term by \(c1=0\). Then choose \(c0,c4\). Matches.
25. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + A c2 e^{c3/(c4+t)}\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
26. \(A^{1/3}c0 + \sqrt(A)c1 + c2 e^{c3 t}\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
27. \(\sqrt(A)c0 + c1|A|^{1/3} + c2 e^{c3 t}\): set \(c2=0\). Then choose \(c0,c1\). Matches.
